# Geometrodynamics

**A research framework implementing and testing Wheeler's geometrodynamic program.**

This package computationally explores the hypothesis that structures
physicists call electromagnetism, charge, spin, confinement, **black
holes**, and **Bell correlations** may emerge from the geometry of
spacetime itself ÔÇö specifically the Hopf fibration on S┬│, 5D Tangherlini
wormholes, topological flux-tube networks, coherent wormhole-throat
condensates, and non-orientable throat topology.

## Direction of the program: GR Ôćĺ QFT, *not* quantum gravity

**BAM derives quantum field theory *from* continuous (classical) general
relativity ÔÇö it is the opposite of a quantum-gravity program, and does not
attempt to quantise gravity.** The foundation is a *classical*, continuous GR
geometry: the wormhole throat, the 5D Tangherlini bulk, the metric `f(r)`. The
quantum field theory ÔÇö the matter spectrum, the propagator/exchange kernel, the
self-energy, the interaction vertices (PRs #116, #129ÔÇô#140) ÔÇö is the *derived*
output, obtained as standard field theory **on that fixed classical background**.

So the arrow runs **geometry Ôćĺ fields**, never **fields Ôćĺ geometry**:

  - the metric is a classical input, never a quantised dynamical field;
  - "throat", "horizon", "5D Tangherlini" name a *classical GR background*, and
    the probes that build propagators, vertices, and self-energies are deriving
    *QFT on that background*, in the precise sense of QFT-on-curved-spacetime;
  - asking BAM to "tackle quantum gravity" is therefore a **category error** ÔÇö
    it would invert the program. Gravity here is the foundational *classical*
    layer from which quantum matter is reconstructed, not a thing to be
    quantised.

When the probes below speak of the path-integral measure `S_BAM`, the
one-loop determinant, or the bounded interacting vacuum, these are statements
about the **matter QFT** read off the classical throat geometry ÔÇö not about a
quantum theory of the metric.

## Where ÔäĆ enters: scale-free closure ledger + one geometric anchor

The closure-ledger arc (`experiments/closure_ledger/`, PRs #11ÔÇô#74)
reduces every dimensionless parameter in the locked lepton surrogate
to closure-quantum invariants (`action_base = 2¤Ç`, `transport = 8¤Ç`,
`resistance = 7¤Ç/100`, `pinhole ╬│ = ╬ú V_max[1..5]`, `╬▓_lepton = k_5┬▓┬Ě(2¤Ç) = 50¤Ç`,
`╬Á = 7¤Ç/(100┬Ěk_5Ôü┤)`), and an audit (`maslov_dimensional_bridge_probe`,
PR #52) then established that the machinery is **scale-free**:
rescaling `R_MID Ôćĺ ╬╗┬ĚR_MID` leaves every dimensionless output
invariant. By dimensional analysis, **exactly one external dimensionful
anchor is mathematically required** (B4 is irreducible). The Compton
bridge then collapses to

```
ÔäĆ  =  m_e ┬Ě R_MID ┬Ě c              (equivalently  m_e = f_closure ┬Ě ÔäĆ / (╬öR┬Ěc))
```

That anchor need not be a particle mass: it is **relocatable to the
invariant bulk separation** `╬öR = R_OUTER Ôłĺ R_INNER` (PR #53,
`delta_r_scale_modulus_probe`), a cosmologically fixed length (the
throat is a static bound vacuole, decoupled from Hubble flow), with
`f_closure = ╬öR/R_MID = 0.52`. The chain
**imposed `R_MID` Ôćĺ invariant geometric length `╬öR` Ôćĺ finite-self-energy
equilibrium** has each step more physical (PRs #55ÔÇô#58):
`self_consistent_throat_radius_probe` recasts `R*` as a stable
equilibrium `E(R) = A/R + B┬ĚR┬▓` of EM repulsion vs cohesion (`U_EM/(mc┬▓) = ╬▒/2`,
no UV divergence); `cohesive_tension_derivation_probe` derives
`B = 4¤Ç¤â` as the throat brane tension (the unique `R┬▓` power by
power-counting); `brane_tension_tuning_probe` sharpens the bulk-gravity
relation to the **exact** RS fine-tuning `╬╗_crit = ÔłÜ(6|╬ŤÔéů|)/╬║Ôéů┬▓`
(dimensionless factor ÔłÜ6, the flat / static-throat condition); and
`pair_production_threshold_probe` makes `2 m_e c┬▓` the lowest stable
configuration (one Hopf charge per throat Ôćĺ C-conjugate
throatÔÇôantithroat pair).

**Scaffold status:** four of five mismatch terms (B1, B2, B3, B5) closed;
B4 audited as irreducible-by-dimensional-necessity. Full ledger:
`docs/bam_scaffold_status.md`. Release note:
`docs/scaffold_closure_release_note.md`.

**Reproduce in seconds:**

```bash
python -m experiments.closure_ledger.maslov_dimensional_bridge_probe
# Verdict: B4_IRREDUCIBLE ÔÇö scale-free invariance verified.
```

## Why progress is possible beyond Wheeler's geometrodynamics

Wheeler's original geometrodynamic programme had the right *instinct*
ÔÇö that what we call "matter" should ultimately be a property of
spacetime itself ÔÇö but it stalled in the 1960s and 70s for a concrete
reason: it lacked the **global / topological machinery** needed to
turn that instinct into a quantitative spectrum.  The continuum
Einstein equations alone do not pick out discrete spectra; they
admit far too many solutions.  Wheeler's "charge without charge" and
"mass without mass" remained slogans precisely because there was no
mechanism to make them *count* anything.

The line continued here is concrete: discreteness arises from three
independent topological/geometric channels, all of which can be
written down explicitly and integrated numerically.

1. **Antipodal S┬│ closure.**  Compactifying the spatial slice as
   S┬│ replaces the open continuum with a closed cavity, so any
   field that closes on itself does so over a great circle of fixed
   length 2¤Ç.  Resonance on a closed cavity is intrinsically
   discrete; the closure constants (`action_base = 2¤Ç`, the
   integer-winding lock `4╬▓ = 100┬Ě(2¤Ç)` for the ¤ä lepton) are
   *exact* topological invariants of this antipodal closure.  The
   closure constants are not fitted; they are read off from the
   global structure.
2. **Non-orientable throat/shell spectra.**  A wormhole throat
   that is non-orientable carries a ZÔéé partition class (`p = ┬▒`)
   which is a real topological label, not a continuous parameter.
   The unique orientation-reversing isometry of S┬│ that preserves
   the Hopf bundle is `T = i¤â_y` (derived in `embedding/transport.py`
   without ansatz).  T┬▓ = ÔłĺI is the 4¤Ç periodicity of spinors; the
   partition splitting drives every mass-ordering inversion in the
   shelled sector (the m_u < m_d but m_c > m_s pattern).  The
   throat orientation is what makes spin-┬Ż unavoidable rather
   than imposed.
3. **Uniform bulk distance from outer to inner.**  The throat
   confines a radial coordinate to the finite shell `[R_INNER,
   R_OUTER]` (geometric units; throat at `R_MID = 1`).  In tortoise
   coordinates this becomes a finite interval with regular
   boundary conditions, which produces a discrete eigenmode
   spectrum (`tangherlini.radial.solve_radial_modes`) ÔÇö bound
   modes `u_{l,n}(r*)` with frequencies `¤ë(l,n)`.  This is the
   bulk geometry's own quantization channel, independent of the
   S┬│ closure but composing with it.

What was missing in Wheeler's day ÔÇö and what this package now
demonstrates operationally ÔÇö is that these three channels **compose**.
The lepton ladder is a "minimal closure" spectrum where channel 1
(S┬│ closure) dominates: each lepton mass scales with its global
pass-count winding `╬▓┬Ěk┬▓` on a nearly bare closure skeleton, locked
by `4╬▓_lepton = 100┬Ě(2¤Ç)`.  The quark ladder (added in this work)
is a "shell-coupled closure" spectrum where channel 1 picks up the
heaviest shell only and channels 2 and 3 ÔÇö partition asymmetry on
the throat and bulk-mode coupling ÔÇö determine the lighter shells.
Three of the four quark-sector residuals derive from
`tangherlini.radial.solve_radial_modes` and
`tangherlini.alpha_q.derive_alpha_q` to within 1%, on the same
tortoise grid that defines the radial bound modes (see
`docs/quark_axioms.md` ┬ž8 for the full derivation log and the
quantitative match per residual).

This is what allows progress: the right machinery for *quantitative*
geometrodynamics exists, it is just not the differential-geometric
machinery Wheeler had at hand.  Antipodal closure on a compact 3-space,
non-orientable throat topology, and bulk-mode confinement are each
old and individually well understood; what is new here is putting
them together and showing that they reproduce charged-lepton masses
to sub-percent and the six-quark mass ladder to ~1.6%.

| The hard `S_BAM` path-integral measure: full loop-measure construction | **Structurally defined; analytic core open** | Takes up PR #74's flagged open work ÔÇö builds the full measure `Z = ╬ú_sectors Ôłź D╬╝[X] e^{ÔłĺS_BAM[X]}` around the `1/(2¤Ç)` factor. **Arena:** loop space `LS┬│ / (Diff S┬╣ Ôőë U(1)_Hopf Ôőë ZÔéé)`, `D╬╝ ~ ╬á dk/(2¤Ç)`. **Fixed (computable):** closure quantum `2¤Ç` = loop holonomy; superselection sectors = the closure ledger (homotopy `k`, `cÔéüÔłł¤ÇÔéâ(S┬▓)=ÔäĄ`, `n_part`); **odd-k lemma UPGRADED to the ZÔéé orientation-anomaly condition** `e^{ik¤Ç}=Ôłĺ1 Ôč╣ k odd` (even `k` = torus cover only); the PRs #87ÔÇô#90 bounces = the leading saddle. **Hard part:** `Diff(S┬╣)` gauge-fixing Ôč╣ FP(`bc`-ghost) ├Ś fluctuation-det; the fluctuation operator (= 2nd variation of `S_BAM` = Tangherlini cavity operator) is stable (min `¤ë┬▓Ôëł1.11>0`). **Open:** the bare determinant `╬á ¤ë_n` diverges (log-det Ôćĺ Ôł×) Ôč╣ needs zeta/heat-kernel regularization; `Z` not yet rigorously constructed. Prior saddle results (leading `e^{ÔłĺS}`) unaffected (`s_bam_path_integral_measure_probe`, PR #115) |
| Regularize the Tangherlini fluctuation determinant | **Analytic core CLOSED ÔÇö finite, two ways** | Resolves PR #115's open one-loop factor: the divergent bare `╬á_n ¤ë_n` is regularized to a **finite, scheme-independent** value by two independent standard methods that agree. **Gel'fandÔÇôYaglom** (no mode sum ÔÇö one IVP solve): `det(H)/det(H_free) = y(L)/L = 1.57437` (log `0.45386`), converged to 6 digits `N = 2000 Ôćĺ 32000`, zero interior nodes (no negative modes). **Zeta/heat-kernel:** `╬Â(0) = aÔéÇ = Ôłĺ1/2` (the universal Dirichlet-interval value ÔÇö finite, no zero mode, no anomaly), Weyl leading coeff `a_{Ôłĺ1/2} Ôëł L/ÔłÜ(4¤Ç)` to 0.9%, counting `N(╬╗) Ôëł (L/¤Ç)ÔłÜ╬╗` confirmed. The `S_BAM` one-loop measure factor is finite and computable. **Still open:** closed-form expression (the value is numerical) and the absolute `Z` normalization (the `╬║Ôéů┬▓/╬ŤÔéů` anchor, PR #112) (`tangherlini_fluctuation_determinant_probe`, PR #116) |
| Diff(S┬╣) FaddeevÔÇôPopov / ghost determinant | **Gauge sector complete ÔÇö finite, anomaly-free** | Supplies the measure's gauge sector (PR #115 flagged it; PR #116 did matter). | **Two-throat HartreeÔÇôFock sandbox** ÔÇö direct plus exchange terms | **Convolves the #186 hardened overlap kernels with an interaction to build the OVERLAP-NORMALIZED two-throat HF energy `E┬▒(R)=(J(R)┬▒K_ex(R))/(1┬▒S┬▓)` ÔÇö the orbital overlap `S=ÔčĘ¤ć_a\|¤ć_bÔčę`, the DIRECT (Hartree) numerator `J=ÔłźÔłź¤ü_a¤ü_b V` and the EXCHANGE numerator `K_ex=ÔłźÔłź¤ä¤äV` (`¤ä=¤ć_a¤ć_b`) all from the actual #180 throat-soliton orbitals; `J, K_ex` are the unnormalized HF numerators and `(1┬▒S┬▓)` the overlap normalization. **The integrals** (3D-FFT Coulomb on the #180 orbitals): `S(R)={0:1.0,1:0.79,2:0.41,3:0.15,4:0.05}`, `J(R)={0:0.039,1:0.031,2:0.017,ÔÇŽ}`, `K_ex(R)={0:0.039,1:0.024,2:0.006,ÔÇŽ}` ÔÇö all positive (repulsive `V`), decaying, the direct dominating (`K_ex/J` from 1.0 at contact to ~0.01 at R=4). **The normalized energies & fermion ordering (repulsive V):** `E┬▒=(J┬▒K_ex)/(1┬▒S┬▓)`; for the repulsive screened interaction the antisymmetric (fermion) branch `EÔéő` sits BELOW the symmetric (boson) `EÔéŐ` at every finite separation (`R=1: EÔéő=0.019<EÔéŐ=0.034`; `R=2: 0.014<0.020`; `R=3: 0.008<0.009`) ÔÇö the exchange hole lowers the GR-selected antisymmetric (PinÔü╗) state, the gap closing as the overlap `SÔćĺ0` (distinguishable, nearly degenerate); the ordering is SCOPED to a repulsive `V` (an attractive interaction reverses it; and the normalization itself works against it ÔÇö dividing `EÔéő` by `1ÔłĺS┬▓<1` raises it ÔÇö yet the fermion branch stays lower across the tested range). **Pauli at coincidence (the zero vector):** as `RÔćĺ0`, `SÔćĺ1` and BOTH the numerator `JÔłĺK_exÔćĺ0` AND the normalization `1ÔłĺS┬▓Ôćĺ0` ÔÇö the antisymmetric combination `╬ĘÔéő=(¤ć_a¤ć_bÔłĺ¤ć_b¤ć_a)/ÔłÜ(2(1ÔłĺS┬▓))` is the ZERO VECTOR, i.e. FORBIDDEN (two identical fermions cannot occupy the same orbital), **not** a state with zero interaction energy; the boson `EÔéŐ=(J+K_ex)/(1+S┬▓)` survives (bunching). For a CONTACT `V` the numerator `JÔłĺK_ex=0` at all R (`J=K_ex=g┬ĚD(R)`, the hardened #186 direct overlap), so `EÔéő=0` at every finite separation (the exchange exactly cancels the direct ÔÇö the Pauli hole removes the contact interaction), the state forbidden only at exact coincidence. **Controls + convergence:** at far separation `S,J,K_exÔćĺ0` (orthogonal, distinguishable throats, `EÔéŐÔëłEÔéő`); under 3D-grid refinement `N=64Ôćĺ80Ôćĺ96` the energies converge to `<0.1%` (the precise values carry the #186 soliton-profile ~3% uncertainty). **Scope:** a SANDBOX ÔÇö rigid #180 orbitals (the self-consistent two-throat HF solve is a follow-up), a screened-photon (Yukawa) regulated stand-in for the BAM Coulomb/photon `1/q┬▓` interaction (#42ÔÇô#44), spatial (orbital) exchange only (the spin/statistics factor is the separate PinÔü╗ `Ôłĺ1`), energies in code units; the overlap-normalized structure (S(R), the direct/exchange numerators, the `(1┬▒S┬▓)` normalization, fermion-lower for a repulsive V, and the forbidden zero-vector antisymmetric state at coincidence) is robust; weak-field (`two_throat_hartree_fock_probe`, PR #187) |

the deformations are within the orientability/spin-preserving class (a genuine topology change is outside the smooth family by construction); this establishes robustness, not a re-derivation of #174; | **The phase-slip / topology-change event** ÔÇö exactly how the invariant changes when q hits zero | **Dissects the one event that changes the discrete charge: the topological OBSTRUCTION (changing Q forces an exact zero ÔÇö a straight homotopy winding-1Ôćĺwinding-0 is driven through `min\|q\|=2.5├Ś10Ôü╗┬╣ÔüĚ` at `s*=0.5, ¤ć*=¤Ç`), the QUANTUM (across a simple zero `╬öQ=┬▒1`, the integrated `Ôł«Ôłç¤ć` changing by exactly Ôłĺ2¤Ç), and the DYNAMICS (Q(t) is a quantized staircase whose every step coincides with a `min\|q\|Ôćĺ0` event); away from the zeros Q is an exact integer (to 10Ôü╗┬╣ÔüÁ) ÔÇö the invariant is ambiguous ONLY at amplitude zeros** | Resolves the #181 handle (the unsustained winding driven to `\|q\|=0` slips) into the full anatomy of the topology-change event. **The obstruction:** Q is a homotopy invariant of `q:S┬╣ÔćĺÔäéÔłľ{0}`, so to change it the field MUST leave `ÔäéÔłľ{0}` ÔÇö the straight homotopy `(1Ôłĺs)┬Ě[winding 1]+s┬Ě[winding 0]` is FORCED through an exact zero (`min\|q\|=2.5├Ś10Ôü╗┬╣ÔüĚ` at `s*=0.5`, located at `¤ć*=¤Ç`), where Q jumps 1Ôćĺ0; there is no nowhere-zero path between sectors (the dynamical content of the #175 gate). **The quantum:** across that simple zero `╬öQ=Ôłĺ1` exactly ÔÇö the integrated winding density `Ôł«Ôłç¤ć` changes by `Ôłĺ2¤Ç` (one full turn of phase removed at the zero point); the winding is an integer before and after, ambiguous only AT the zero. Cross-checks the 0╬Ż╬▓╬▓ prediction (one spectrum) (`cosmological_sigma_mnu_probe`, PR #96) |
| meV-scale spectrum **sharpened** (NuFIT 6.0 + DESI DR2) | **Pinned; only ╬úm_╬Ż testable** | Sharpens the #96 band into a full pinned spectrum. NuFIT 6.0 fixes `mÔéé = 8.65`, `mÔéâ = 50.34 meV` (NO floor `╬úm_╬Ż = 59.0`); DESI DR2 + CMB (Ôë▓60ÔÇô64 meV) corners `mÔéü Ôë▓ 3 meV` Ôč╣ **`╬úm_╬Ż Ôłł [59.0, 62.6] meV`** (tightened from 59ÔÇô65, toward the floor). Lab effective masses: `m_╬▓ Ôëł 8.8ÔÇô9.3 meV`; **`m_╬▓╬▓` has a nonzero floor `[1.5, 3.7] meV`** ÔÇö NO contributions can't fully cancel (`s12┬▓c13┬▓mÔéé = 2.60 > s13┬▓mÔéâ = 1.10 meV`). **Honest reachability:** only `╬úm_╬Ż` is near-term testable (DESI, at the floor now); `m_╬▓` ~4ÔÇô5├Ś below Project 8, `m_╬▓╬▓` ~3ÔÇô10├Ś below LEGEND-1000/nEXO. Flag: some 2025 DESI+CMB fits prefer ╬úm_╬Ż at/below the floor Ôćĺ tension for all NO models (`neutrino_mev_scale_sharpening_probe`, PR #111) |

### Research goals (not yet fully derived)

| Physics | Proposed geometry |
|---------|-------------------|
| Electromagnetism | Curvature of the Hopf connection on S┬│ |
| Charged-lepton ladder (e, ╬╝, ¤ä) | Eigenvalues of a k-pass instanton-transition matrix with S┬│ action base `2¤Ç` and k=5 uplift `200¤Ç` ÔÇö **sub-percent fit achieved** |
| Particle mass (general) | One Bohr-Sommerfeld closure operator `m┬▓ = (S/L_eff)┬▓` over both fermion sectors: leptons = throat-winding (`k Ôëá 0`), quarks = cavity-resolving (`k = 0`); inter-generation hierarchy still open (PR #83) |
| QCD confinement | 1D flux-tube network with bridge nucleation ÔÇö Cornell `¤âLÔłĺA/L` audited (PR #99): flux tube = wormhole bridge, string breaking = PR #58 Schwinger throat-pair (`eEÔćĺ¤â`); `ÔłÜ¤â` the one QCD anchor |
| Retrocausal photon exchange | WheelerÔÇôFeynman absorber theory on S┬│ |
| Black-hole interior | Coherent condensate of non-orientable wormhole throats |
| Bell correlations | Non-orientable throat transport + Hopf SU(2) projection |
| Entanglement = wormholes | Bell correlations from throat connectivity |
| Quantisation from resonance | S┬│ antipodal cavity selecting discrete spectrum |
| Topological censorship | Non-orientable throats evading standard no-go theorems |
| QFT event reinterpretation (Compton) | Antipodal `S┬│` Green function as propagator + Hopf-fibre photon polarisation + closed-form vertex resummation reproducing Klein-Nishina exactly ÔÇö see [QFT-event-reinterpretation thread](#qft-event-reinterpretation-thread-compton-scattering) below |

## Installation

```bash
git clone https://github.com/davidmdrpi/geometrodynamics.git
cd geometrodynamics
pip install -e ".[dev]"
```

## Running the Validation Suite

```bash
# All tests (fast)
pytest

# Include slow tests (bridge nucleation, string tension scans)
pytest -m ""

# Skip slow tests
pytest -m "not slow"
```

## Lepton mass ladder (e, ╬╝, ¤ä) from a locked S┬│ action

The lepton surrogate now ships with a **fully locked topological baseline**
that reproduces all three charged-lepton masses to sub-percent accuracy with
**zero free parameters at scan time** ÔÇö only the electron mass is used to set
the overall MeV scale.

### Locked axioms

- `action_base = 2¤Ç`  ÔÇö the S┬│ great-circle action (circumference invariant).
- `k_uplift_beta = 50¤Ç`  ÔÇö k-selective uplift coefficient.
  For `k=5`, the uplift is `4┬Ě╬▓ = 200¤Ç`, i.e. **exactly 100 ├Ś (2¤Ç)** S┬│
  winding quanta.
- `winding_mode = "max"`  ÔÇö off-diagonal tunneling cost scales with the deeper
  branch, `╬ök = max(kßÁó, kÔ▒╝)`.
- `depth_cost_mode = "tunnel_only"`  ÔÇö the S┬│ base action enters only through
  the tunneling suppression, not as an additional diagonal offset.
- `resistance_model = "exponential"`  ÔÇö re-entry cost `╬║┬Ě(eßÁĆ Ôłĺ 1)` captures
  exponential geometric writhe/curvature build-up with generation depth.
- Baseline anchor `(phase, transport, pinhole, resistance) Ôëł
  (0.001, 25.1, 22.5, 0.217869)`. As of the closure-ledger sequence
  (`docs/hbar_origin_note.md`), all four are now identified with
  closure-quantum / Tangherlini-grid invariants:
  `transport = 8¤Ç`, `pinhole ╬│ = ╬ú V_max[1..5]`,
  `resistance = 7¤Ç/100`, with the phase channel decoupled.

The generation-block diagonal takes the form

```
H_kk = action_base + resistance_scale ┬Ě k┬▓  +  res_diag(k)
                  +  pinhole(k Ôłł {3, 5})   +  ╬▓ ┬Ě max(0, kÔłĺ3)┬▓
```

and off-diagonals are `Ôłĺtransport ┬Ě exp(Ôłĺ╬▒_eff ┬Ě ╬ök) ┬Ě cos(phase ┬Ě ╬ök)`.
See `docs/lepton_axioms.md` for the full matrix construction.

### Validated predictions (locked baseline, no tuning)

| Lepton | k | Predicted (MeV) | Observed (MeV) | Relative error |
|--------|---|-----------------|----------------|----------------|
| e      | 1 | 0.510999        | 0.510999       | 0.0000% (anchor) |
| ╬╝      | 3 | 105.61260       | 105.65838      | **0.0433%** |
| ¤ä      | 5 | 1778.93809      | 1776.86        | **0.1170%** |

Muon/electron ratio: predicted **206.6787**, observed **206.7683**
(relative error **4.33 ├Ś 10Ôü╗Ôü┤**).

Reproduce directly from Python:

```python
from geometrodynamics.tangherlini import solved_lepton_masses_mev
masses = solved_lepton_masses_mev()           # read-only np.ndarray
print(masses)   # [0.51099895, 105.6126..., 1778.9381...]
```

Or by CLI (no `PYTHONPATH` needed):

```bash
python scripts/lock_beta_50pi_probe.py --n-points 32
```

which additionally pins `╬▓ = 50¤Ç` exactly and optimizes only the four
sub-leading knobs; it reports `mu/e` error Ôëł 1 ├Ś 10Ôü╗ÔüÂ% and
`¤ä` relative error Ôëł 0.161%.

### Geometric implications

1. **Three generations correspond to odd pass depths `k = 1, 3, 5`.** The
   ladder is labelled by the number of S┬│ passes before closure; the locked
   baseline scans exactly these three depths. **Even-`k` absence is now
   classified** as a spin-statistics selection rule (`even_k_absence_probe`,
   PR #67): `k mod 2` is the orientability/spin-statistics grading
   (`T^k` off-diagonal for odd `k` = orientation-reversing closure across
   the non-orientable throat = spin-┬Ż fermion; diagonal for even `k` =
   orientable double cover = bosonic). Charged leptons are spin-┬Ż, hence
   the odd class. The sharp upper bound `k ÔëĄ 5` is the
   **three-generation boundary** (`three_generation_boundary_probe`, PR
   #70), and `k_5 = 5 = D_bulk = dim(S┬│) + 2` is the BAM bulk dimension
   (`k5_origin_probe`, PR #73), with `╬▓_lepton = k_5┬▓┬Ě(2¤Ç) = 50¤Ç`
   (`beta_lepton_derivation_probe`, PR #71) and `#generations = (k_5+1)/2 = 3`
   (`three_throat_modes_probe`, PR #72) both derived from the same `k_5`
   primitive.
2. **¤ä uplift is exactly 100 quanta of the S┬│ action.** The k=5 uplift is
   `4╬▓ = 200¤Ç = 100┬Ě(2¤Ç)`, a pure integer multiple of the great-circle action
   `2¤Ç`. No tuning is required; removing the integer lock degrades `¤ä` by an
   order of magnitude (see `docs/lepton_tau_target.md`).
3. **The ╬╝/e ratio is a structural eigenvalue ratio, not a coupling.** With
   `action_base = 2¤Ç` locked and the exponential resistance profile, the
   calibration scan finds exact ╬╝/e roots on a broad resistance basin
   (┬▒1% resistance keeps `mu_err` < 8%), replacing the earlier
   "attractor needle" regime (see `docs/lepton_tau_target.md`, "Hard S┬│ lock
   experiment").
4. **Quadratic diagonal `ÔłŁ k┬▓` plus quadratic uplift `ÔłŁ (kÔłĺ3)┬▓`** together
   reproduce the observed `m_e : m_╬╝ : m_¤ä Ôëł 1 : 207 : 3477` hierarchy: the
   `k┬▓` term sets the `╬╝/e` split and the `(kÔłĺ3)┬▓` term independently lifts
   the ¤ä sector without disturbing the `╬╝/e` root.
5. **Tunneling-side depth cost dominates diagonal depth cost.** The ablation
   scan showed `tunnel_only` outperforms `diag_only` by nearly 2├Ś on best
   ╬╝/e (see `docs/lepton_ablation_results.md`) ÔÇö consistent with a picture in
   which the inter-generation transition amplitude, not the on-generation
   mass term, sets the ratio.
6. **A `max` winding rule beats a `delta` winding rule.** Setting
   `╬ök = max(kßÁó, kÔ▒╝)` (rather than `|kßÁó Ôłĺ kÔ▒╝|`) in the tunneling action was
   the change that first pushed `╬╝/e` from ~10 toward the experimental
   ~206.77, because it penalises transitions into deeper branches by the full
   target winding ÔÇö a topological-cost interpretation consistent with the S┬│
   action base.

### Script map

| Script | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `scripts/calibrate_muon_ratio.py` | Coarse grid; solves resistance for exact ╬╝/e root at each (phase, transport, pinhole). |
| `scripts/sweep_k_uplift_beta.py`  | Sweeps `╬▓` with exact ╬╝/e enforced; locates best ¤ä fit. |
| `scripts/map_basin_k_uplift.py`   | Local gradient probe around an exact-╬╝/e point; reports basin width. |
| `scripts/refine_locked_tau.py`    | Dense locked scan with action_base fixed to 2¤Ç; reports integer-winding ╬▓ family. |
| `scripts/lock_beta_50pi_probe.py` | Hard `╬▓ = 50¤Ç` lock; optimizes only (phase, transport, pinhole, resistance). |

See `docs/lepton_ablation_results.md`, `docs/lepton_tau_target.md`, and
`docs/lepton_next_steps.md` for the full scan archaeology, and
`docs/hbar_origin_note.md` for the closure-ledger reduction of the
locked surrogate's parameters to closure-quantum invariants.

## Quark mass ladder (u, d, s, c, b, t) from a shell-coupled S┬│ closure

Parallel to the lepton sector, the six observed quark masses are
fit by a 6├Ś6 Hermitian Hamiltonian on the closure basis
`{(k=1,┬▒), (k=3,┬▒), (k=5,┬▒)}`.  The minimal v3 ansatz did not
suffice; three opt-in structural extensions (`uplift_mode =
"partition_asymmetric"`, `spectrum_zero_mode = "min_eigenvalue"`,
`chi_q_k3`, `eta_k3k5_minus`), all with defaults that recover
the minimal lepton-style ansatz, give the locked spectrum.

### Locked spectrum (d-anchor, max rel err 1.6%)

Anchored on `d = 4.67 MeV`; `u` is at zero by construction under
min-eigenvalue spectrum zero.

| species | predicted (MeV) | observed (MeV) | rel err |
|---------|----------------:|---------------:|--------:|
| u | 0           | 2.16    | 1.00 (by construction) |
| d | 4.67        | 4.67    | 0 (anchor)             |
| s | 94.82       | 93.4    | **1.5%**               |
| c | 1290.92     | 1270    | **1.7%**               |
| b | 4219.92     | 4180    | **0.95%**              |
| t | 170342.41   | 172690  | **1.4%**               |

### Locked parameters (constraint-reduced)

The full residual sector is *derivable from existing geometry*
on the eigensolver's tortoise grid:

| sector | reading |
|--------|---------|
| `action_base = ¤Ç` | structural |
| `uplift_asymmetry ╬Á = 1 Ôłĺ 1/k_5┬▓ = 24/25` | partition asymmetry from inverse-square shell scaling |
| `eta_k3k5_minus ╬Ě = k_5 = 5` | (3,Ôłĺ)ÔÇô(5,Ôłĺ) targeted off-diagonal coupling |
| `chi_q_k3 ¤ç = (k_5 Ôłĺ 1)┬Ěk_5 = 20` | k = 3 partition splitter |
| `phase = 0` | partition-mixing channel inactive at the lock |
| `gamma_q = 1/10` | empirical clean rational |
| `transport Ôëł 0.54` | mean `ÔčĘu_l\|V_{l+2}ÔłĺV_l\|u_{l+2}Ôčę` on tortoise grid (+0.87% off) |
| `pinhole Ôëł 22.25` | `╬ú_{l=1..5} V_max(l)` on tortoise grid (Ôłĺ1.09% off) |
| `resistance Ôëł 0.14` | `transport ┬Ě ln(╬▒_q(k_5)/╬▒_q(k_1))` (Ôłĺ0.43% off) |
| `╬▓ = N ┬Ě ¤Ç/2 with N=466` | **remaining phenomenological parameter** |

### Shell-coupled vs minimal closure

The diagonal-Hamiltonian decomposition shows what makes the
quark ladder structurally distinct from the lepton ladder:

| species | ╬▓ contribution |
|---------|---------------:|
| u, d (k=1) | 0% |
| s         | +11% (level mixing only) |
| c         | **Ôłĺ27%** (pushed *down* by level repulsion) |
| b         | +76% via ╬▓┬Ě4┬Ě(1Ôłĺ╬Á) = ╬▓┬Ě4/k_5┬▓ |
| t         | **+99%** via ╬▓┬Ě4┬Ě(1+╬Á) Ôëł ╬▓┬Ě4┬Ě(49/25) |

`╬▓` only enters at the heaviest shell (k=5), via the
partition-asymmetric `(1┬▒╬Á)` factor.  The lighter shells (u, d,
s, c) are determined entirely by the chamber-coupling sector
(pinhole, ¤ç, ╬│_q).  This is the operational signature of the
"shell-coupled closure" picture: the same S┬│ closure skeleton
that drives the lepton ladder is, in the quark sector, primarily
expressed through how the closure interacts with an interior
chamber rather than through global pass-count winding.

### Calibration archaeology

| Script | Purpose |
|--------|---------|
| `scripts/calibrate_quark_ratios.py` | Coarse grid over the residual sector; identifies ╬│_q regime where positivity holds. |
| `scripts/sweep_quark_beta.py` | Integer-winding ╬▓ sweep (now known to be a fit knob, not a topological lock). |
| `scripts/map_basin_quark_uplift.py` | Basin probe around the best ╬▓. |
| `scripts/lock_quark_beta_probe.py` | Final lock with ╬▓ hard-fixed (legacy from the integer-N attempt). |
| `scripts/experiment_partition_asymmetric_uplift.py` | Tests the k=5 b/t splitter. |
| `scripts/experiment_min_eigenvalue_zero.py` | Tests d-anchor with min-eigenvalue spectrum zero. |
| `scripts/experiment_k3_splitter.py` | Tests ¤ç for the c/s splitter. |
| `scripts/experiment_refined_k3k5.py` | Pass-2 refinement crossing the user-named "serious candidate" threshold (max rel err < 0.3 Ôćĺ 0.13). |
| `scripts/basin_probe_topological_locks.py` | Verifies N, ¤ç, ╬Ě are basin features, not grid coincidences. |
| `scripts/refine_pass3_coord_descent.py` | Coordinate-descent refinement to 1.6%. |
| `scripts/experiment_constraint_search.py` | Constraint-reduction pass: 9 free knobs Ôćĺ 4 + 1. |
| `scripts/experiment_n_ablation.py` | First N-stability check (residuals free); N drifts. |
| `scripts/experiment_residuals_from_geometry.py` | Substitutes residuals with broad geometric scalars. |
| `scripts/experiment_transport_pinhole_search.py` | 1D refinement of transport and pinhole derivations. |
| `scripts/experiment_transport_overlap.py` | Derives transport from QM perturbation overlap to within 0.87%. |
| `scripts/experiment_resistance_wkb.py` | WKB tunneling-derived resistance (negative result), then discovers `resistance = transport ┬Ě ln(╬▒_q ratio)` to within 0.43%. |
| `scripts/experiment_n_ablation_geometric.py` | Decisive N-stability check with all residuals derived; N still drifts Ôćĺ ╬▓ is phenomenological. |

See `docs/quark_axioms.md` (full v3 spec, calibration log ┬ž8,
phenomenological interpretation ┬ž9) and the JSON archive in
`docs/calibration_runs/` for the raw outputs of every scan.

## QFT-event-reinterpretation thread (Compton scattering)

An 11-PR thread (PRs #25 ÔÇô this PR) testing whether BAM's three
composable dynamical elements ÔÇö **throat worldlines + time dilation
at mouth + antipodal closure** ÔÇö reproduce QFT event structure for a
canonical local interaction, Compton scattering `╬│ + e Ôćĺ ╬│ + e`. The
thread progressively identified the BAM-native ingredients needed
to reproduce Klein-Nishina, then resummed the perturbative result
into a closed-form vertex factor.

### Result chain

  - **Kinematics** (PR #25): closure-compatible. The antipodal map
    `(E, **p**) Ôćĺ (E, Ôłĺ**p**)` automatically conserves the
    back-vertex when the front does. Inter-mouth proper-time skew
    vanishes; throat-pinch skew is a recoil-induced `O(¤ë┬▓/m┬▓)`
    quantity, not a topological closure quantum.

  - **Propagator** (PR #26): the `S┬│` Green function
    `G(¤ł) Ôł╝ 1/(4¤Ç¤ł)` with `¤ł = (s Ôłĺ m┬▓)/(2m┬▓)` reproduces the QED
    propagator pole `1/(s Ôłĺ m┬▓)` exactly (fitted exponent 1.0002).

  - **Photon structure** (PR #28): giving the photon two transverse
    polarisations on the `S┬│` tangent bundle and treating the
    electron as a scalar charge in the Thomson limit reproduces
    `(1 + cos┬▓╬Ş)/2` exactly ÔÇö the full Klein-Nishina angular factor.

  - **Finite-energy gap** (PR #29): the natural BAM construction
    fails at `O(¤ë/m)`. The recoil sign is qualitatively wrong
    (BAM enhances backscatter, KN suppresses it), localised to the
    missing per-channel kinematic weighting.

  - **Vertex coupling** (PRs #30, #31): an extended Family B vertex
    modification `V = (╬Á┬Ě╬Á'*)┬Ě(1 + ╬Á┬Ě╬╝Ôéü + ...)` with
    `╬╝Ôéü = ╬│┬Ě(¤ë/m)┬Ě(1 Ôłĺ cos ╬Ş)` closes the `O(╬Á)` gap exactly at
    `╬│ = Ôłĺ3/2` ÔÇö derived analytically from a 4-equation linear
    system over `{1, c, c┬▓, c┬│}` basis.

  - **Coefficient origin** (PRs #32, #33): 8 natural BAM ingredients
    evaluate to `Ôłĺ3/2`; the dimensional-scaling test in `d Ôłł {3, 4,
    5, 6}` falsifies the embedding-dim / polarisation-count origin
    (candidate C), leaving 7 surviving candidates rooted in
    group-theoretic invariants of SU(2).

  - **`O(╬Á┬▓)` extension** (PR #34): polynomial leading-order
    closure with `(╬ŻÔéÇ, ╬ŻÔéü, ╬ŻÔéé, ╬ż) = (9/4, Ôłĺ4, 7/4, Ôłĺ1/2)`, with
    structural patterns `╬ŻÔéÇ = ╬│┬▓ = (Ôłĺ3/2)┬▓` (recursive) and
    `╬ż = ÔłĺA_¤ć(0)` (Hopf-charge link).

  - **Resummation** (PR #35): the closed form

      F┬▓(x, c) = 4┬Ěx┬│┬Ě(x┬▓ + 1 Ôłĺ x┬Ěsin┬▓╬Ş) / [(1 + c┬▓)┬Ě(1 + x)┬▓]
              = (2x/(1+x))┬▓ ┬Ě [x┬Ě(x┬▓+1Ôłĺx┬Ěsin┬▓╬Ş) / (1+c┬▓)]

    with `x = ¤ë'/¤ë = 1/(1 + ╬Á(1 Ôłĺ cos ╬Ş))` reproduces Klein-Nishina
    **exactly at all orders in ╬Á up to ╬Á ~ 2** (machine precision).
    The perturbative results of PRs #31ÔÇô34 are Taylor expansions
    of this closed form.

  - **Cross-process validation via BreitÔÇôWheeler** (this PR): the
    same closed-form F, expressed in Lorentz invariants and
    analytically continued via standard Mandelstam crossing
    (`s_C Ôćĺ u_BW`, `t_C Ôćĺ s_BW`, `u_C Ôćĺ t_BW`), exactly reproduces
    the BreitÔÇôWheeler pair-production amplitude `╬│╬│ Ôćĺ eÔü║eÔü╗`.
    Crossed variables `x_ÔŐŚ = Ôłĺ(1Ôłĺ╬▓┬Ěcos╬Ş)/(1+╬▓┬Ěcos╬Ş) < 0` and
    `c_ÔŐŚ = (2╬▓┬▓ Ôłĺ ╬▓┬▓cos┬▓╬Ş Ôłĺ 1)/(1Ôłĺ╬▓┬▓cos┬▓╬Ş)` carry the construction
    from Compton lab kinematics to BW CM kinematics; the
    BAM-predicted `|M╠ä|┬▓_BW = Ôłĺ2┬Ě(f_baseline ┬Ě F┬▓)/x_ÔŐŚ┬▓` agrees
    with the textbook formula to machine precision at all sampled
    `(╬▓, cos╬Ş)`, and the integrated differential reproduces the
    textbook BW total at threshold (`╬▓ Ôćĺ 0` linear) and in the
    ultra-relativistic regime (`╬▓ Ôćĺ 1` logarithmic). The vertex F
    is therefore **not a Compton-specific algebraic fit** ÔÇö it is
    the closed form of the invariant QED amplitude carried by
    crossing to its tree-level partners.

### Structural reading

The `(1 + c┬▓)` denominator in the angular factor IS the
polarisation-sum factor. The closed-form F must be derived AS a
modification of the polarisation-sum projector, not as a separate
amplitude factor. The two-factor decomposition

  - kinematic Pad├ę `(2x/(1+x))┬▓` ÔÇö pure x-function
  - angular polarisation modification `[x┬Ě(x┬▓+1Ôłĺx┬Ěsin┬▓╬Ş) / (1+c┬▓)]`

suggests two BAM-native ingredients combine to produce the full
vertex coupling. The clean half-integer/integer rationals appearing
at every order (╬│ = Ôłĺ3/2, ╬ŻÔéÇ = 9/4, ╬ŻÔéü = Ôłĺ4, ╬ŻÔéé = 7/4, ╬ż = Ôłĺ1/2)
indicate a deeper geometric origin awaiting first-principles
derivation from the Hopf-bundle / throat-transport algebra.

### What survives and what is still open

  - Survives: BAM's antipodal-`S┬│` propagator + Hopf-fibre photon
    polarisation + closed-form vertex `F┬▓` together reproduce
    Klein-Nishina exactly. The same closed form, crossed via
    Mandelstam permutation, reproduces BreitÔÇôWheeler `╬│╬│ Ôćĺ eÔü║eÔü╗`
    (PR #36) and pair annihilation `eÔü║eÔü╗ Ôćĺ ╬│╬│` (this PR); the full
    Compton/BW/annihilation crossing triangle closes (loop is
    identity at both the Mandelstam-label and amplitude level).
  - Open: first-principles BAM derivation of `F┬▓` from a BAM
    Lagrangian / action. Two-channel tree processes (Bhabha, M├Şller)
    with interfering s+t diagrams; loop corrections requiring the
    bulk radial channel.

**Synthesis / release note:** `docs/tree_qed_status.md` collects the
PR #35 Ôćĺ #46 result ÔÇö all tree-level `2 Ôćĺ 2` QED scalar intensities
(Compton, BreitÔÇôWheeler, pair annihilation, Bhabha, M├Şller)
reproduced from BAM-geometric primitives.

The Compton derivation rests on the algebraic identity

  x┬▓ + 1 Ôłĺ x┬Ěsin┬▓╬Ş Ôëí (1 Ôłĺ x)┬▓ + x ┬Ě (1 + c┬▓)

which yields two equivalent decompositions:

  F┬▓(x, c) = [2x/(1+x)]┬▓ ┬Ě [x┬▓ + x┬Ě(1Ôłĺx)┬▓/(1+c┬▓)]
  |M╠ä|┬▓_KN/(8eÔü┤) = (1+c┬▓) + (1Ôłĺx)┬▓/x

with BAM-geometric interpretation:

  - **P(x) = 2x/(1+x)** = harmonic mean of in/out photon frequencies
    = standard classical bottleneck-flux average through the throat;
    squared because both throat-pair mouths pinch. Uniquely
    polynomial ÔÇö alternative throat-rates (arithmetic, geometric mean,
    linear x) leave Q non-polynomial at x Ôćĺ Ôłĺ1.
  - **(1+c┬▓)/2 = cosÔü┤(╬Ş/2) + sinÔü┤(╬Ş/2)** = sum of squared Wigner-d┬╣Ôéü,┬▒Ôéü
    matrix elements = Hopf-fibre spin-1 helicity transport through ╬Ş.
  - **Q = |a|┬▓ + |b|┬▓** = orthogonal sum of helicity-preserving
    (a = x) and helicity-flipping (b = ÔłÜx(1Ôłĺx)/ÔłÜ(1+c┬▓)) channels,
    each non-negative across the physical region.
  - The Hopf connection at the BAM lock `A_¤ć(0) = 1/2` (from
    `geometrodynamics.hopf.connection`) matches the PR #34 perturbative
    coefficient `╬ż = Ôłĺ1/2` exactly.
  - Decomposition survives analytic continuation under crossing
    (full Compton Ôćö BW Ôćö annihilation triangle, PR #37).

The full F┬▓ closed form is derived from three foundational
principles via a single BAM throat action functional (PR #41):

  (P1) closure quantum `S = 2¤Ç` (BAM `action_base`)
  (P2) S┬│ antipodal symmetry `¤â(p) = Ôłĺp` (involution swapping mouths)
  (P3) stationary action under the antipodally-symmetric ansatz

Both equal-action postulates (PR #39 energy Ôćĺ K, PR #40 spin/Hopf Ôćĺ Q)
follow as consequences. Alternative principles (broken antipodal
symmetry; wrong closure quantum; wrong action functional) all fail
to reproduce K(x), confirming the principles are necessary.

The thread then extends to 4-fermion tree QED (Bhabha, M├Şller,
PRs #42ÔÇô#46): SU(2) Hopf-bundle Pauli traces give the Dirac-trace
diagonal numerators (#43), the non-orientable throat transport
`T = i¤â_y = ╬Á` gives the Fermi-statistics interference signs (#44),
and the `S┬│` Green function (scalar #45, Hopf-bundle vector #46)
gives the photon propagator `1/q┬▓` with full Lorentz tensor
structure. End-to-end Bhabha and M├Şller `|M╠ä|┬▓` match QED to machine
precision from BAM-geometric ingredients alone.

See `docs/tree_qed_status.md` for the full synthesis. Per-PR
research plans: `docs/compton_vertex_resummation_research_plan.md`
(#35), `docs/breit_wheeler_cross_process_research_plan.md` (#36),

### BAM effective-action scaffold ÔÇö barrier closure (PRs #49ÔÇô#53)

The tree-QED ingredients above were assembled into a single covariant
5D effective-action scaffold and its five mismatch terms (B1ÔÇôB5) were
worked off one by one. Four are now **closed**:

| barrier | what it was | now |
|---|---|---|
| **B1** closure quantum `Ôł«A = 2¤Çn` | imposed constraint | winding ╬Ş-term `S_top = 2¤Ç┬Ěn` |
| **B2** antipodal `ZÔéé` (`T = i¤â_y`) | imposed identification | `RP┬│ = S┬│/ZÔéé` + non-trivial spin structure |
| **B3** hard-wall throat BC | imposed by hand | single-valuedness under `T┬▓ = ÔłĺI` Ôč╣ `¤ł(throat) = 0` |
| **B5** 5DÔćĺ4D reduction producing F┬▓ | unconstructed | one master functional yields masses **and** `F┬▓=K┬▓┬ĚQ` |

B5 is closed by the **master integral**: a single separable functional
on the warped-product internal geometry `M_int = C ├Ś S┬│`
(`C` = radial cavity `[R_MID, R_OUTER]`),

```
Ôä│(¤ë; x, c) = G_C(r, rÔÇ▓; ¤ë) ÔŐŚ ­Łĺó_{S┬│}(╬ę, ╬ęÔÇ▓)
```

read three ways from one object ÔÇö

  - **poles in ¤ë** Ôćĺ the mass spectrum `¤ë(l,n)` (radial ladder `n` ├Ś
    S┬│ Casimir `l`, the centrifugal term of the warp);
  - **throat boundary of `G_C`** Ôćĺ `K(x) = 2x/(1+x)` (dwell-time
    impedance `Z(¤ë)=¤Ç/¤ë` in series);
  - **S┬│ Hopf reduction of `­Łĺó_{S┬│}`** Ôćĺ `Q(x,c) = x┬▓+x(1Ôłĺx)┬▓/(1+c┬▓)`
    (Hopf-fibre helicity spinor).

The vertex residue reproduces `F┬▓(x,c) = K┬▓┬ĚQ` to machine precision
(`2e-14`) while the poles give the masses ÔÇö **masses and the full
vertex from one functional**. The `F┬▓=K┬▓┬ĚQ` factorization is the direct
consequence of the product internal geometry (separation of variables),
not a failure to unify.

The fifth barrier **B4** (the dimensional bridge `ÔäĆ = m_e┬ĚR_MID┬Ěc`) is
not a gap but a **structural necessity**: the closure-ledger/Maslov
machinery is *scale-free* (rescaling `R_MID Ôćĺ ╬╗┬ĚR_MID` leaves every
dimensionless output invariant), so exactly one external dimensionful
anchor is mathematically required ÔÇö **B4 is irreducible** (#52). That
anchor need not be a particle mass: it can be the **invariant bulk
separation** `╬öR = R_OUTER Ôłĺ R_INNER`, a proper (cosmologically fixed)
length, giving `m_e = f_closure┬ĚÔäĆ/(╬öR┬Ěc)` with `f_closure = 0.52` (#53).
The scaffold is therefore complete: four barriers derived, the fifth the
single mandatory dimensionful unit. Full ledger:
`docs/bam_scaffold_status.md`; closure release note:
`docs/scaffold_closure_release_note.md`; per-probe plans:
`docs/topological_discrete_sector_research_plan.md` (#49),
`docs/radial_reduction_bridge_research_plan.md` (#50),
`docs/bulk_boundary_interaction_research_plan.md` and
`docs/master_integral_research_plan.md` (#51),
`docs/maslov_dimensional_bridge_research_plan.md` (#52),
`docs/delta_r_scale_modulus_research_plan.md` (#53).

### Pati-Salam bridge + mass-operator unification (PRs #82ÔÇô#83)

| arc | PRs | summary |
|---|---|---|
| **Throat Ôćö shell `n+3` bridge** | #82 | Each generation has a lepton at `n = gÔłĺ1` (throat) and a quark-pair at `n = g+2` (shell); shift `+3` = PR #68 shell threshold (no free parameter). Unified 12-state `(l, n, p)` basis + throat-shell ZÔéé. Full SU(4) PS needs 3 open extensions: BAM-native neutrinos, 3-fold quark color, **lepton-quark mass-operator unification**. |
| **Bohr-Sommerfeld mass-operator unification** | #83 | The third extension is **closed at the structural-form level**: the lepton `╬▓┬Ěk┬▓` (PR #71) and quark `¤ë┬▓(l,n)` (PR #77) mass operators are the SAME Bohr-Sommerfeld operator `m┬▓(k,n) = (k┬Ě2¤Ç/L_throat)┬▓ + ((n+1)┬Ě¤Ç/L_cavity)┬▓`, `L_throat = ÔłÜ(2¤Ç)/k_5`. Cavity `Ôł«ÔłÜ(¤ë┬▓ÔłĺV)dr* = (n+1)┬Ě¤Ç` verified to machine precision; `(2¤Ç/L_throat)┬▓ = k_5┬▓┬Ě(2¤Ç) = 50¤Ç = ╬▓_lepton` recovered. |

**The unification, in one line.** Leptons and quarks are not two kinds
of object with two mass formulas. They are **one Bohr-Sommerfeld
closure operator** `m┬▓ = (S/L_eff)┬▓` read in two channels of the
closure ledger (PR #52's `N_total = N_layer1 + N_radial`):

  - **Leptons wind through the throat** ÔÇö winding number `k Ôłł {1,3,5}`,
    closure quantum `2¤Ç` (full S┬│ great circle) Ôćĺ `m┬▓ Ôëł ╬▓┬Ěk┬▓`.
  - **Quarks resolve the cavity** ÔÇö `k = 0` (no throat traversal),
    radial overtone `n Ôłł {3,4,5}`, closure quantum `¤Ç` (half-cycle
    Bohr-Sommerfeld node) Ôćĺ `m┬▓ Ôëł ¤ë┬▓(l, n)`.

The user's physical insight ÔÇö *"quarks do not pass through the throat;
they are the wavefronts that resolve the cavity itself"* ÔÇö is exactly
`k = 0` in this single operator. The `2¤Ç`-vs-`¤Ç` distinction between the
two channels is BAM's pervasive full/half-cycle structure (throat dwell
`¤ä = ¤Ç/¤ë`, Hopf holonomy `Ôł«A = ¤Ç cos ¤ç`, B3 reflection phase `¤Ç`).
What remains open: an independent derivation of the two `L_eff` from one
principle, and the inter-generation hierarchy (the cross-channel /
mixed-mode question).

### Neutrino & full-quadrant sector (PRs #85ÔÇô#87)

With the lepton/quark mass operator unified (PR #83), the `(k, n)`
plane splits into four quadrants, and the chargeless `k = 0` corner
turns out to be the neutrino ÔÇö the long-open "BAM-native neutrino"
extension of the Pati-Salam bridge (PR #82).

| arc | PRs | summary |
|---|---|---|
| **Four-quadrant map / leptoquark** | #85 | The unified `(k, n)` operator's fourth quadrant (winding **and** shell-saturated, `kÔëá0, nÔëą3`) is the **leptoquark** sector, completing the reading: lepton `(kÔëá0, n<3)`, quark `(k=0, nÔëą3)`, neutrino `(k=0, n<3)`, leptoquark `(kÔëá0, nÔëą3)`. |
| **Neutrino = Majorana seesaw** | #86 | The `(k=0, n<3)` quadrant gives the lightest states but ~10ÔüÁÔÇô10ÔüÂ too heavy. The fix is BAM-native: `k=0 Ôč╣ cÔéü=0 Ôč╣ C-invariant` (PR #63) Ôč╣ the neutrino is its own antiparticle Ôč╣ **Majorana**, so it admits the seesaw `m_╬Ż = m_D┬▓/M_R`. The seesaw is available **only** to the chargeless sector ÔÇö charged leptons (`cÔéü=┬▒1`) are Dirac and keep their full winding mass ÔÇö which is precisely why only neutrinos are anomalously light. Required `M_R Ôëł 0.3ÔÇô1.8 TeV` was left open (no BAM scale at ~TeV). |
| **`M_R` from throat-nucleation tunnelling** | #87 | The `╬öL=2` Majorana coupling **is** the PR #58 throatÔćöantithroat (antipodal `ZÔéé`) transition, and PR #58's `╬úcÔéü=0` applied to a single state **is** PR #86's only-neutrino selection rule (`k=0` flips `0Ôćĺ0`, allowed; `kÔëá0` gives `╬úcÔéü=Ôłô2`, forbidden). The literal `M_R = `barrier-height hypothesis is **falsified** ÔÇö with the electron-throat `¤â, ¤ü` the barrier is `E_c Ôëł 2.8 keV`, ~10ÔüŞ too small. Instead the suppression is **tunnelling through** the barrier, `m_╬Ż = m_D┬Ěe^{ÔłĺS}`, so `M_R = m_D┬▓/m_╬Ż = m_D┬Ěe^{S}`: the ~TeV scale is the keV Dirac floor exponentially lifted, and the open input is recast from a mysterious ~TeV mass to a modest, generation-stable bounce action `S Ôëł 15ÔÇô18` ÔÇö exactly the instanton-rate follow-on PR #58 flagged. |
| **Bounce action `S` = non-orientable tortoise log** | #88 | A reduced Euclidean bounce `S = ÔłÜ(2 ╬╝ E_c)┬ĚL*(╬Á)` for the flip, run along the odd (`cÔéüÔćĺÔłĺcÔéü`) tortoise path. The 5D tortoise coordinate diverges logarithmically at the throat, giving two structural results: a **rigid throat Ôč╣ exactly massless neutrino** (the boundary compliance `╬Á` is the mass-generating parameter, and the smallness of `m_╬Ż` is the near-rigidity of the throat), and `S ÔłŁ ln(1/╬Á)` ÔÇö naturally `O(10)` and generation-stable, the form PR #87 required. **Honest magnitude:** the EM-throat tension under-produces `S` by ~40├Ś (`S Ôë▓ 1` even near-rigid); matching `S Ôëł 15ÔÇô18` needs a `╬öL=2` (BÔłĺL) throat tension `~6ÔÇô12├Ś` stiffer. The open input is localised once more: ~TeV mass (#86) Ôćĺ `O(15)` action `S` (#87) Ôćĺ `O(10)` BÔłĺL/EM tension ratio (#88). |
| **BÔłĺL tension ratio bracketed by closure & winding** | #89 | The `╬öL=2` flip reverses orientation (`cÔéüÔćĺÔłĺcÔéü`) ÔÇö a **global** operation ÔÇö so `t` is a global-closure enhancement of the **local** EM surface tension. It is bracketed, parameter-free, by the two basic BAM action scales: the **closure quantum `2¤Ç`** (a single great-circle orientation reversal, lower) and the **winding action `k_5ÔłÜ(2¤Ç) = ÔłÜ╬▓_lepton`** (a full throat winding, upper), giving `t Ôłł [2¤Ç, k_5ÔłÜ(2¤Ç)] Ôëł [6.28, 12.53]` ÔÇö **exactly** PR #88's required `6ÔÇô12` (the computed `[6.41, 12.05]` sits inside). So the `6ÔÇô12` band was not a fit but the BAM closure-to-winding window. The residual is "where in the window" = the compliance `╬Á` (`t=2¤Ç Ôč╣ ╬ÁÔëł6e-7`, `t=ÔłÜ╬▓ Ôč╣ ╬ÁÔëł1.3e-2`); the winding/cavity mass ratio `m_charged/m_D Ôëł 11.9 Ôëł ÔłÜ╬▓` corroborates the winding edge. |
| **Compliance `╬Á` from bulk geometry Ôćĺ `m_╬Ż` scale** | #90 | The capstone. `╬Á` is the chargeless throat's sub-throat **healing length** (`╬Á = Ôäô┬▓/2rs` from the neck warp `fÔëł2(rÔłĺrs)/rs`), sub-throat *for the neutrino* because the `cÔéü=0` neck has no EM term to prop it open (the charged `cÔéü=┬▒1` neck is propped open and stays Dirac) ÔÇö the same chargelessness that makes the neutrino Majorana makes its `╬Á` tiny, hence its mass tiny. Natural BAM sub-throat scales (`R_c┬│, ╬ö┬│, (m_D/m_ch)┬▓`) land `╬Á` in the PR #89 window; with the winding-edge tension `tÔëłÔłÜ╬▓` (cross-check-favoured) the chain gives `S Ôëł 15ÔÇô19` and **`m_╬Ż ~ few meV`** ÔÇö the observed scale, with no input outside the throat geometry. At the `2¤Ç` edge `SÔëł4` (too small): the chain closes only at the winding edge. |
| **Generation spread + `PMNS Ôëź CKM`** | #91 | Generations are the cavity radial overtones `n`, so the bare prediction is **normal ordering** with `m_╬Ż ÔłŁ m_D` (cavity-floor ratios `1:1.87:2.74`). The spread is widened in the right direction by the overtone-dependent neck coupling ÔÇö PR #79's boundary stress `¤ç_n` decreases with `n` (0.304, 0.097, 0.039), so higher-`n` neutrinos are less throat-coupled Ôč╣ more compliant Ôč╣ less suppressed Ôč╣ relatively heavier (lifting `mÔéâ` toward the observed spread). **Headline:** large PMNS vs small CKM is the BAM **cross-channel** (leptons: charged throat-winding `kÔëá0` ├Ś neutrino cavity-resolving `k=0`) vs **intra-channel** (quarks: up & down both cavity-shell `k=0`) distinction ÔÇö the structural reason `PMNS Ôëź CKM`. Precise spectrum (`╬Á_n(¤ç_n)` `O(1)`, absolute scale unmeasured) and explicit angles open. |
| **PMNS anarchic vs CKM aligned (quantitative)** | #92 | Computes the cross-channel overlap. A naive radial overlap gives near-permutation (small) mixing ÔÇö large PMNS is *not* a literal mode overlap. The lepton generation labels live in **different coordinates** (charged: closure-winding `k`; neutrino: radial-overtone `n`), so the map has no preferred alignment Ôč╣ **anarchic** (Haar-random). Observed PMNS (33.4┬░, 49┬░, 8.6┬░) is **typical** of a Haar `U(3)` (30th/57th/4th percentile); CKM (13┬░, 2.4┬░, 0.2┬░) is **extremely atypical** (joint `p Ôëł 0`) = aligned ÔÇö up & down share the radial-overtone (shell) coordinate. So PMNS Ôłł anarchy class (cross-coordinate), CKM Ôłł aligned class (intra-coordinate) ÔÇö a falsifiable separation matching observation. Specific angles not pinned (anarchy is statistical; ╬Ş13 at the 4th percentile is the mild tension). |
| **╬Ş13 suppression / residual alignment** | #93 | Resolves the PR #92 ╬Ş13 tension. ╬Ş13 = `U_e3` is the corner element ÔÇö it links the lowest winding (`k=1`) to the highest overtone (`n=2`), the most coordinate-distant (**two-hop**) pair ÔÇö while ╬Ş12, ╬Ş23 are adjacent (one hop). Since the throatÔćöshell coupling is **local** in the `(k,n)` lattice (PR #82 `+3` shift, PR #83 operator), the corner is a suppressed two-hop amplitude ÔÇö a residual **nearest-neighbour** alignment. A structured-anarchy model (corner variance `exp(Ôłĺ╬╝)`, `╬╝=0` = pure anarchy) with `╬╝Ôëł3` shifts the ╬Ş13 distribution down (median 33┬░Ôćĺ~16┬░), makes ╬Ş13 robustly the *smallest* angle (frac 0.50Ôćĺ0.72), and moves observed ╬Ş13=8.6┬░ from the 4th to the ~21st percentile ÔÇö **tension resolved** ÔÇö while ╬Ş12 (~44th) and ╬Ş23 (~70th) stay typical. The exact value (╬╝; ╬Ş13 median saturates ~14ÔÇô16┬░) is open. |
| **CP / Majorana phases** | #94 | The phase sector. **CP violation is generic**: the winding amplitudes carry the Hopf holonomy `e^{ik¤ç}` (PR #60), so the cross-channel overlaps are intrinsically complex and `╬┤_CP Ôëá 0, ¤Ç` with probability 1 (CP conservation is measure-zero). The **Jarlskog invariant** mirrors the angle dichotomy: `|J_PMNS| Ôëł 0.026` is typical of anarchy (51st/81st percentile Ôćĺ large CP violation), `|J_CKM| Ôëł 3├Ś10Ôü╗ÔüÁ` is extremely atypical (~0.1th Ôćĺ aligned/suppressed). And the **two Majorana phases exist** because the neutrino is Majorana (`cÔéü=0`, PR #86) ÔÇö CP phases of the ╬öL=2 throatÔćöantithroat sector (PRs #87ÔÇô#90), observable in 0╬Ż╬▓╬▓; a Dirac neutrino would have none. The specific phase values are anarchic (uniform) ÔÇö not pinned (`╬┤_CP` is itself poorly measured, consistent with uniform). |
| **0╬Ż╬▓╬▓ effective mass** | #95 | Turns the whole arc into one falsifiable number-range. The effective Majorana mass `m_╬▓╬▓ = |╬ú U_ei┬▓ m_i|` combines: 0╬Ż╬▓╬▓ **occurs** (neutrino Majorana ÔčŞ `cÔéü=0`, PR #86; Dirac would forbid it); **normal ordering** (PR #91) selects the NO band (`m_╬▓╬▓ Ôëł 1.5ÔÇô3.7 meV` at zero lightest mass); **anarchic Majorana phases** (PR #94) populate the full band incl. a cancellation trough (`m_╬▓╬▓ Ôćĺ ~0` around `m_lightest ~ 3ÔÇô5 meV`); and the **light scale** (PR #90, ~few meV) gives `m_╬▓╬▓ Ôë▓ 8 meV`. This sits below the current bound (KamLAND-Zen 28ÔÇô122 meV ÔÇö null result expected), largely below next-gen reach (LEGEND-1000 / nEXO ~9ÔÇô20 meV), and below the inverted-ordering floor (~19 meV). **Sharp falsifier:** a 0╬Ż╬▓╬▓ discovery with `m_╬▓╬▓ Ôë│ 19 meV` would imply inverted ordering or a quasi-degenerate scale, contradicting the BAM normal-ordering + light-scale prediction. |
| **Cosmological ╬úm_╬Ż** | #96 | The cosmological companion to #95: the same light, normal-ordered spectrum fixes `╬úm_╬Ż = m1+m2+m3`. The NO floor is `ÔłÜ╬öm┬▓_21 + ÔłÜ╬öm┬▓_31 Ôëł 58.7 meV` (the IO floor Ôëł 99 meV), and the light scale (PR #90, ~few meV) keeps the sum pinned near it: **`╬úm_╬Ż Ôëł 59ÔÇô65 meV`**. This is consistent with Planck 2018 + BAO (<120 meV), just inside DESI DR1 + CMB (<72 meV), and **right at the DESI DR2 + CMB frontier (~60ÔÇô64 meV)** ÔÇö exactly where current cosmology is probing. **Falsifiers:** a robust `╬úm_╬Ż < 58.7 meV` excludes normal ordering (and is in tension with the oscillation `╬öm┬▓` themselves); a quasi-degenerate `╬úm_╬Ż Ôë│ 100 meV` contradicts the light scale. `╬úm_╬Ż` and `m_╬▓╬▓` (#95) are one spectrum's two observables ÔÇö a joint, cross-checkable prediction. |

**Where it lands.** The neutrino sector is now structurally complete:
the only-neutrino-Majorana selection rule, the seesaw mechanism, and a
BAM-native home for the seesaw scale (the throatÔćöantithroat nucleation
tunnelling) are all in place. The headline is the reframing: **`M_R` is
no longer a free ~TeV mass but an instanton action**. Because
`M_R = m_D┬Ěe^{S}`, the entire 6-order gap between the keV Dirac floor
and the TeV seesaw scale is carried by a single dimensionless number
`S Ôëł 15ÔÇô18` ÔÇö the Euclidean bounce/instanton action for the `╬öL=2`
throatÔćöantithroat tunnelling. PR #88 then builds that bounce explicitly
and shows it is the **non-orientable tortoise logarithm**: a rigid
throat gives an exactly massless neutrino, and `S ÔłŁ ln(1/╬Á)` is
naturally `O(10)` and generation-stable. PR #89 then constrains the
remaining tension ratio: because the flip reverses orientation it is a
*global* operation, so `t` is bracketed parameter-free by the **closure
quantum `2¤Ç`** and the **winding action `k_5ÔłÜ(2¤Ç) = ÔłÜ╬▓_lepton`** ÔÇö
`t Ôłł [6.28, 12.53]`, exactly PR #88's required `6ÔÇô12`. The open input
has now been localised four times ÔÇö ~TeV mass (#86) Ôćĺ `O(15)` action
(#87) Ôćĺ `O(10)` tension ratio (#88) Ôćĺ the BAM closure-to-winding window
(#89) ÔÇö leaving a single residual number: *where in that window*, i.e.
the boundary compliance `╬Á`. PR #90 closes the chain: `╬Á` is the
chargeless throat's sub-throat **healing length** (`╬Á = Ôäô┬▓/2rs`), tiny
*for the neutrino* precisely because its `cÔéü=0` neck is not propped open
by charge ÔÇö the same chargelessness that makes it Majorana. With the
winding-edge tension the natural bulk scales give `S Ôëł 15ÔÇô19` and
**`m_╬Ż ~ few meV`**, the observed scale, with no input outside the
throat geometry. So the whole chain ÔÇö `~TeV` mass Ôćĺ `O(15)` action Ôćĺ
`O(10)` tension ratio Ôćĺ closure-to-winding window Ôćĺ sub-throat healing
length Ôćĺ `meV` ÔÇö is closed at order-of-magnitude: **the neutrino mass
scale is geometric, not tuned.** PR #91 then takes up the spread and the
mixing: generations are the cavity overtones, so the bare prediction is
normal ordering with `m_╬Ż ÔłŁ m_D`, widened in the right direction by the
overtone-dependent neck coupling (PR #79's `¤ç_n` falls with `n`, so
higher-`n` neutrinos are less suppressed, hence heavier). And the
long-standing `PMNS Ôëź CKM` puzzle is the **cross-channel vs
intra-channel** distinction: leptons mix across the throat-winding
(`kÔëá0`) / cavity-resolving (`k=0`) divide ÔÇö large; quarks mix within the
single cavity-shell channel ÔÇö small. What remains open is the precise
neutrino spectrum (an `O(1)` coefficient; the absolute scale is
unmeasured ÔÇö only `╬öm┬▓`) and the explicit mixing angles. PR #92 takes up
the angles and finds the cross-channel structure is **anarchic**: because
the charged-lepton generation lives in the closure-winding coordinate and
the neutrino generation in the radial-overtone coordinate ÔÇö different,
unaligned coordinates ÔÇö the PMNS matrix is effectively Haar-random, and
the observed angles (33.4┬░, 49┬░, 8.6┬░) are *typical* of that anarchic
distribution, while CKM is *extremely atypical* (aligned, joint
`p Ôëł 0`), as expected for up/down quarks sharing the one shell
coordinate. The class-level separation (PMNS anarchic, CKM aligned) is a
firm BAM prediction; the specific angles, being statistical, are not
pinned (╬Ş13 sitting on the small side is the one mild tension). PR #93
resolves that last tension: ╬Ş13 = `U_e3` is the corner element ÔÇö the
lowest winding (`k=1`) ├Ś highest overtone (`n=2`), the most
coordinate-distant pair ÔÇö so it is reached by *two* channel-hops, and a
residual nearest-neighbour alignment (the throatÔćöshell coupling is local
in the `(k,n)` lattice) suppresses that two-hop amplitude. This makes ╬Ş13
robustly the smallest angle and moves the observed value from the 4th to
the ~21st percentile, with ╬Ş12, ╬Ş23 staying typical ÔÇö leaving only the
exact value (one residual-alignment parameter) and the CP/Majorana phases.
PR #94 closes that last item structurally: CP violation is **generic**
(the winding amplitudes carry the complex Hopf holonomy `e^{ik¤ç}`, so the
PMNS is generically complex and CP conservation is measure-zero), the
Jarlskog invariant mirrors the angle dichotomy (`|J_PMNS|` typical of
anarchy, `|J_CKM|` extremely atypical/aligned), and the **two Majorana
phases exist** because the neutrino is Majorana (`cÔéü=0`, PR #86) ÔÇö
observable in 0╬Ż╬▓╬▓, with none for a Dirac neutrino. The phase *values*,
like the angles beyond the dichotomy, are anarchic and not pinned. With
this, the neutrino arc (#85ÔÇô#94) closes: the sector's *structure* ÔÇö
Majorana nature, mass scale, ordering, mixing class, ╬Ş13 hierarchy, CP
genericity, Majorana-phase existence ÔÇö is BAM-native, while the precise
spectrum and the specific phases/angles remain the (statistical /
one-parameter) residuals. PR #95 then collapses that structure into a
single falsifiable observable, the 0╬Ż╬▓╬▓ effective Majorana mass: 0╬Ż╬▓╬▓
*occurs* (Majorana), in *normal ordering*, with *anarchic phases* and a
*light scale*, giving `m_╬▓╬▓ Ôë▓ 8 meV` (with cancellation to ~0) ÔÇö below
current bounds and the inverted-ordering floor (~19 meV), so a discovery
at `m_╬▓╬▓ Ôë│ 19 meV` would falsify the prediction. The neutrino sector thus
ends not just structurally complete but with a concrete experimental
target for next-generation tonne-scale 0╬Ż╬▓╬▓ searches. PR #96 adds the
cosmological companion from the *same* spectrum: `╬úm_╬Ż Ôëł 59ÔÇô65 meV`,
pinned at the normal-ordering floor and sitting right at the DESI DR2 +
CMB frontier (~60ÔÇô64 meV) ÔÇö so the two flagship neutrino observables,
`m_╬▓╬▓` (Ôë▓ 8 meV) and `╬úm_╬Ż` (~60 meV), are a joint, cross-checkable pair
that current and near-term experiments are now testing.

## Quick Start

### Verify charge quantisation from pure geometry

```python
from geometrodynamics.hopf import compute_c1

result = compute_c1()
print(f"|cÔéü| = {result['c1_abs']:.10f}  (error: {result['err_abs']:.2e})")
# |cÔéü| = 1.0000000000  (error: 9.99e-14)
```

### Verify spin-┬Ż from Hopf holonomy

```python
from geometrodynamics.hopf import compute_spinor_monodromy

result = compute_spinor_monodromy()
print(f"ÔčĘ¤łÔéÇ|U(2¤Ç)|¤łÔéÇÔčę = {result['overlap_2pi']:.6f}  (should be Ôłĺ1)")
print(f"ÔčĘ¤łÔéÇ|U(4¤Ç)|¤łÔéÇÔčę = {result['overlap_4pi']:.6f}  (should be +1)")
```

### Validate Coulomb law from eigenmode throat flux

```python
from geometrodynamics.tangherlini import solve_radial_modes, solve_maxwell_from_eigenmode

modes = {}
for l in [1, 3, 5]:
    oms, fns, rg = solve_radial_modes(l)
    modes[l] = {"omega": oms, "funcs": fns}

result = solve_maxwell_from_eigenmode(modes)
print(f"Q = {result['Q']:.6f}")
print(f"Relative error vs exact Coulomb: {result['rel_err']:.2e}")
```

### Reproduce the full charged-lepton ladder

```python
from geometrodynamics.tangherlini import (
    solved_lepton_masses_mev, S3_ACTION_BASE, TAU_BETA_50PI, tau_uplift_2pi_quanta,
)

masses = solved_lepton_masses_mev()   # locked baseline, no tuning
print(f"m_e  = {masses[0]:.6f} MeV")
print(f"m_mu = {masses[1]:.6f} MeV   (obs 105.658376)")
print(f"m_tau= {masses[2]:.6f} MeV   (obs 1776.860000)")

print(f"action_base = 2¤Ç         = {S3_ACTION_BASE:.6f}")
print(f"k_uplift ╬▓  = 50¤Ç        = {TAU_BETA_50PI:.6f}")
print(f"¤ä uplift    = 4╬▓ = 200¤Ç  = {tau_uplift_2pi_quanta(TAU_BETA_50PI):.0f} ├Ś (2¤Ç)")
```

### Run a QCD meson simulation

```python
import numpy as np
from geometrodynamics.qcd import make_meson_tube, HadronicNetworkSolver

net = make_meson_tube(L=1.0, v=1.0, N=100, dt=0.004)
s = np.linspace(0, 1.0, 100)
net.initialize_fields(psi0={0: 0.5 * np.sin(np.pi * s)})

solver = HadronicNetworkSolver(net, antipodal_coupling=0.05)
history = solver.run(n_steps=1000, record_every=50)
print(f"Energy drift: {np.std(history['energy']) / history['energy'][0]:.4f}")
```

### Build a black-hole condensate and verify entropy

```python
from geometrodynamics.blackhole import (
    build_schwarzschild_condensate, compute_entropy_balance,
    find_horizons, integrate_radial_geodesic,
)

# Schwarzschild BH as a coherent wormhole-throat condensate
bh = build_schwarzschild_condensate(mass=5.0)
bal = compute_entropy_balance(bh)
print(f"N throats: {bh.N}")
print(f"S_BH  = {bal.S_BH:.2f}")
print(f"S_thr = {bal.S_throat:.2f}  (relative error: {bal.relative_error:.2e})")
print(f"Net charge Q = {bh.net_charge}  (neutral)")

# Nonsingular interior: Hayward metric with core scale from throat network
l = bh.core_scale
horizons = find_horizons(bh.mass, l)
print(f"\nCore scale l = {l:.4f}")
print(f"Horizons: {['%.4f' % h for h in horizons]}")

# Geodesic completeness: infalling worldline decelerates, never hits r=0
geo = integrate_radial_geodesic(M=bh.mass, l=l, r_start=3*bh.mass, tau_max=100)
print(f"Geodesic complete: {geo.is_complete}  (r_min = {geo.r_min:.2e})")
```

## Lineage

This package refactors and unifies three monolithic scripts:

| Original file | Package modules |
|---|---|
| `geometrodynamics_v39.py` | `hopf/`, `tangherlini/`, `transaction/`, `constants.py` |
| `s3_spin2_closure_toy_solver_v22.py` | `tangherlini/` (shared spectral solver) |
| `qcd_topology_solver_v30.py` | `qcd/` (entire subpackage) |
| New in v0.41.0 | `blackhole/` (condensate, interior, entropy, derivation) |
| New in v0.42.0 | `embedding/`, `bell/`, `transaction/cavity.py` |
| New in v0.43.0 | `embedding/transport.py`, `bell/hopf_phases.py`, `history/` |
| New in v0.44.0 | `tangherlini/lepton_spectrum.py` (locked e/╬╝/¤ä ladder) + `scripts/` (calibration CLIs) |
| New in v0.45.0 | `qcd/quark_spectrum.py` + `qcd/hadron_spectrum.py` (shell-coupled six-quark ladder; residual sector geometrized to ~1% via Tangherlini eigenmode) |
| New in v0.46.0 | `experiments/closure_ledger/` (closure-ledger sequence; reduces the locked lepton surrogate's residual external input from six phenomenological parameters to one anchor m_e). Paper draft in `docs/hbar_origin_note.md`. |
| New in v0.47.0 | BAM effective-action scaffold (PRs #49ÔÇô#53): five mismatch terms B1ÔÇôB5; four closed (B1+B2 topological/discrete sector, B3 hard-wall BC, B5 master integral); B4 audited as irreducible-by-dimensional-necessity. Closure release note in `docs/scaffold_closure_release_note.md`. |
| New in v0.48.0 | Throat-as-anchor arc (PRs #55ÔÇô#58): self-consistent equilibrium `R*`, cohesive brane tension `B┬ĚR┬▓`, RS-like ÔłÜ6 brane tuning, pair threshold `2 m_e c┬▓`. |
